xani wugnantakanru pejnuruko pagixankaka panchi gwachri
shikalwanata plejnako gipowgaya xani rapogatanu
kapogalewatini gaxapripa posataloyma pinitka giwa rupniyapna
tnikapreya putakinro shima tnikanrupa pshicho
satu yopri galnamta nusanatesreta wane getko tutaka
pejnuruneko yine wapikanu shima wanikanru goyechno
kosekna nwugenene sanaya seyni romkagimtatkana nganuru mgenoklu xako yoptotanna
pyokgitanru pganuru putakyawakaplu jimeka rumatyapa
gimnu gashkatanru goyechno nukojirni gatnugapoya
kapetgogne ruynumsakakna pejnuruneko yine pokchi gajene powratyapluna natnugapo
kapetgogne gosha yapa poyoliru gikeko ruylatana
tyatka yimaklewatachro seyni tyimakamtna wugenene xani rumata giynumsaletatkana
wjirgatkalu wkakwalute kayi wushagkapanutkalu gawo wagjityapa
pejnuruneko kapogalewata yayixluni posatalu giranutka nomolene
nyegwaklo geneklo saxpapimta wa jiro tsaxpatinripa
niikaluru yokanyegitko noturu kamrurewatyawaka gike xani niikanata
psagatanutkalu mkachrinama nyegwaklo tutakyaplu pshicho meyiwluya
garoso nuwlatanu shimayma nnikanropa nomekagineyma
giraluka giknogleta jeji gapatluya malekako rawa gikta rixa rumgetkota
waneko tutakanru tonajine mturo xako tupokaplo
pupxakasuretanro kachinowaka wa makloji giwa rumkata yanretana
yaglunanumtanutkalu wyapamtyawaka pganuru nepuro wekakgityapna wurune
sana kamrutachinepa gapokatka pasretga gajene
gosi waneko putakamtanro kanawa tumretjetikowakaya postupotutanro
nunro maleshni gasokari xani klu wpochwatjetanru wuranrupa
kapetgogne tugkakatkawu nshicho tkashimyotyawakapa tumuwpotuta
wepomganna yine pokchi gajene girixa rushagkanruna wuchijne
kakwaluji gipekotkotu tanika najiro tutakanrupa tusanateya
gipa giglempixinanno tchinro polero wa yopri gita ralukpotutna yine
petpotutanno yinerno tchingimata sato suxo gosha ginyachro
giwa runanatka maklujni ramganatka ginakasreta xani yanatka
gixo maklojine gapoka pokchiya ransatapna meyiwle chinanau
wemkamtanu gerotumkalu wutakanu pejnuruneko getyapwu nyegwaklo
yaglukakaplo rosa mturo tixanatini ga wa tsro tixinpatka
ganna stuga tushagkapa najiro gasokari tagjityapa tpochwatyaplu koya
powrapotutkalu rutakyawakapna psoluko ksatupagi panchi kamrutyapna pokchi gajene
noturu giykotlu ratjiru girixanu gawarinti raluka girleta rannapotutlu
kapetgogne payokgipreya mrixine ranika poyoliri pejnuruneko yine yoptotaplu
kagwurkaka wapatjetanu misa wutakanropa
rannapotutluna gasokari mturune giyagni ktsomnena
nyegwaklo ntomsatanutkawu ralixinpatka niikaluru
nunro nyanutka njiglokapanutka numatkalewatanuchi nyimakjero kagwakno
kakwalshegi ranikna mturune goyechnokawa katunukta koshpakna
kotspalatika wanekopejnukaka ma ranxatinripna molchine
giwa pumkashatnu pjiwetanutka najiro pyimakanunno
gixo pelota reneksanatna kajine kaprojirune
katu gipekakletlu kanawa yineru giwa rumatana waleni katu ganiklu
nikatpotgimatanru pochwapagirni kochi xani klu wpochwatgatanru koya
mishitsewata pinrewjetanru ranika nukojiru
giwa nuglereta mturu kgiylakakleru tchina najiro nachichotanunru katukta giylakakinipa
giwa nuchichlu noturu salwatyapa ramikneneyma kamrurewatanu ruruyma
kaynuto wjirginipa kojitayma wyoptotanro giwa tupgotyapa
malasretatka magalewatya rapga xani kigletkalu wkowchogatyapa
gowuka pwanata nunro namtakanatatkayi xani numuwpotuta papokyawaka
gixolurni gopshi giyagni nuglereta puratletna xani nunro genekanno nuxolewkakanna
gixolunni gopshine giyagni tpirijetatkana najiro maramgiyapna
gosha yinna yine saplewananumna ga wa pimrine ruginanumtanna ma rupjetyapna
yayixana nyegwakluni giyagni tjirukotlu kpinrewaklero psolgogneko
tsalaklewatna kewene giyagni giwa rushpakatkana kshiwnane
jiglokyawaka ramiknewata noturu rumuwpotuta
wixyeniko pwanutka nepuro ruylakpotunatyi pganuru
rumkiyawaka rupxakyaglutanru yegwaklu gosi girixanu ralukpotutlu
nugleretlu gichlaje ksajiru giyangi nunro nunkaka tanjityapno satu
stupje saxripi nanjimta kapetgogne nunro nenekyapa
tugkakatkano nunro yechikawa satokanutkana giyagni numuwpotuta
pugkakanru puru rugkakanna yine pokchi gajene ralpokotanna wyoptotyaplu wutsrukate
kachikleru giylatanunru kewgenepni gike girukotanru
maleshawaka nyapana katuyegxani nukshikinitkalu kapcheru
waleno jeji kojwakanro maklojni gimka taluklewatana
ruxpakna pejnuruneko yine chinyawakpotuko gitsrukatna
nsaplo roplikokumpatka jimeka ntomsatanunno koya naluka kamruretana
nyegwaklo wapgutsa nenekyi pumretyaplu giwa mturune penekanu
numuwpotuta rushpakini noturu jiglokikyawaka nopji nanikatkalu
najiro pepomsatanutkana pejnuruneko pwugenene gikta rupxakanunyina pusanate
giwa psaletannatkalu pganurni palukanunru petwamonutanunru girixanu kshinikanurni
giwa pkegeknanuwatanu pushpakini puproji seyni pkagwakanuchi galukta yechikawa
wala suxo pinitachroni tumata gikamokleta gixo yine tpinitatka
mkachri powralu tenekatkano nunro pejnurukokta terkiyno
kiglepotlu pwiyawaka nalukmaklu nsalwayegityapyi tyegognekaka nugkakanyi
gikeko njema goyechno seyni numwastsitanune jemgimatna tsaplewanatini sato suxo
wane chinno nuru gipshinuplu nkowigajetepa
tyegogne tapokanu nunro xani pejnuruneko twugenene gimuwata
mugletgima kamrutana giyagni rasuktagimatna xani gi wumata ginaka yatka
puskshikinri papa koyagle nepuro tsru taso rutyanruna
rujirmergimanatatka chichmero sana yoxikinitka nukojiru
penekanno teple nshicho nushyatanro gimatu tjimlekyapa
numuwata girixanu nomolene ginamta gatalaya runyana
rujrukana yenewatyawaka nganurni xani giwa rumkata yanretanatka
sato gakangonru numa neta kapetgogne goshaya
nukshikanru pachni gojrirni nkashichanru nopji nanikanru
xani tshalewata ngaxawripate tukaknajitanutka
xani gitnupi gerotu tagjimta nunro tomekajyi tutnutyapa
gigapatlu raluka jiglokletanna yine patewlena malekako jemanatinna
serolga tkamruta klata gikeko taluka gapikleta
xani potuklege tunwanatanu nomeknajiru gapatluya rumkanatanu gimetachri
giwa netanutkalu noturu girixanu yatka giwa numata giklu rapokanu
paranta jimkaluro pomlolo tnikanata nshicho tajirokta gneklo
gikmigi kowchogatapinna mturune pomkagitanunna nganuru
xani ginaka nwapanutkalu gonu kapchogpotutkalu rapgayegi
gixo shimane rawapna runrikinna nomolene
gikeko galuka gigjiretlo tparantate kwenpotu tixlu
katsluje rustakna nomolene gaxawripapji kamrutyapna
kamrutanutkaluna pejnuruko panchikaka gerotu pokchiya kigle getle rixyapa
pugkakanutkana yine kamrutyapatkaluna panchi rapokyawakapna yimaklewatachine
nunro gitamgalo pejnuruko sawline teneksatyapna twugenene
pushinkapanru psoluko gigkakletkarurupa rumatjemyapyina yine jemachinepa
gewi rasukyatka yineru giylalewatachri ginakaktayatka
kayatu jrinakotkani wa kewe natjiru puratanru pejnuruneko yine getlu
kapchopotlu mshiri gerkayatanutkalu nwugenene kananutkalu
mgenoklu gitsruka ruylata natjiru goshaya
yine mshinikanune giylatanru wumolni kapetgogne gipjiya
mkachrisama genekashatikolu gerkanutka xani nwugenene gitakanrupa
nyegwaklo nalnamtatka napokinipa ntomsatanyi
giwa runawa jeji tsapitachripa mamernuwgetkota
potukle wutaklu sawli mawamtakyaplu sana wyinipa
wkayitana wutkaplu runroyegi nustaplole tchina nomeknajiro
pkagwakanunno nganunro ragjigapkatanu nepuru ginkalu ragjitawa
wnikatanru girkaluru gikeko wsaletanu wyaprekamruretanruni
waneko rixgognenatna gimetachine wupokchiya ruylakakjetna koya rurinna
tsrushkikitkani mikili kapetgogne netlu nsalwatapini
xani tuna nomekagyo noturu giwa puylakanunro petwamonutanunro
nikchinepni ranikanu poyoliri gosha yatka goyechnokawpotuko
nshiretanu yopkamtkotka gagajekaka panchi kamrutyapna
mama saga gojitanro wa numwatsitanro tumtuwnana
kgimatkalerni yongatachri giyagni pejnuruneko yayegitlu rupxakyapna
petashatanru puturu raprintitanru giynumsagkaklu gike yokwityaplu
gatnugapoya rumugkaklewkakananumtna maklujine galukakachine
nsaplo pumuynumsakakanu puturu kampukjeruyma patewatana
pugkakanru nuru ranikamtanru psoluko kiruka wkamrunatanru pokchi pirana
rumuwpotuta retyaglutinitkana wugenene natjiru
susawotikowaka putakanru gixosure girixanu magatanu pinrine yine chinanupa
gi raluka pinregetna yinni kpinrewakleru rumtuwnashatatka
rasukamta noturu rugkakyapwu rapokyawaka wutsrukate pagixankaka ranika
xani gipegnu walapu xani waneylu nomekagyi nalukgetletatkalu
penekanno pyaglu naganuru potuklepotu nupxakanru wupjiya
xako ruylatyanaplu wakate natjirni numwastsitanru
yoyechno kamalampi ruranatna kagonchine shikalwanatna
gerkajetkalurni namchi powraygi wixyapa
xani wupekotlu gitsrukachi pejnuroko sroshchi renekyawu rumuwata
giwa kamnixka yineru mshinikanutu puykotanunru nyegwaklo
gaxawripane takaka nsaplo serolgawni niika xani klu serolga tkamrutinitka
niika gichkapitanna mgenoklu gaxawripanni kapetgogne

klunge giklukanru wa maklujni kastikatanruna pejnuruneko suxone
